//=============================================================================
// AnimSpriteEffect.
//=============================================================================
class AnimSpriteEffect extends Effects;



var() texture SpriteAnim[20];
var() int NumFrames;
var() float Pause;
var int i;
var Float AnimTime;

defaultproperties
{
     DrawScale=+00000.300000
     bUnlit=True
	 bDynamicLight=True
     LightType=LT_Steady
     LightBrightness=199
     LightHue=24
     LightSaturation=115
     LightRadius=20
     bCorona=True
     Physics=PHYS_None
}

//=============================================================================

//=============================================================================

	abstract
	notplaceable;

{
	AutoDestroy=false
}

//*********************************************************
// EmitterBulletTracerGeneric.uc
//
//*********************************************************
class EmitterRain extends Emitter;

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx

const MaxParticlesPerSecond = 300.0;
const InitialIntensity = 0.5;

simulated function PostBeginPlay()
{
	Super.PostBeginPlay();
	Emitters[0].ParticlesPerSecond = MaxParticlesPerSecond * InitialIntensity;
	Emitters[0].InitialParticlesPerSecond = MaxParticlesPerSecond * InitialIntensity;
}

function AdjustRainIntensity( float modifier )
{
	modifier = FClamp( modifier, 0.0, 1.0 );
	Emitters[0].ParticlesPerSecond = MaxParticlesPerSecond * modifier;
	Emitters[0].InitialParticlesPerSecond = MaxParticlesPerSecond * modifier;
}

defaultproperties
{
	Begin Object Class=SpriteEmitter Name=SpriteEmitter28
		UseCollision=false
		UseCollisionOnce=true
		CollisionDistTest=5000
		CoordinateSystem=PTCS_Independant
		DampingFactorRange=(X=(Min=0,Max=0),Y=(Min=0,Max=0),Z=(Min=0,Max=0))
		UseDirectionAs=PTDU_Up
		UseRotationFrom=PTRS_Offset
		UseColorScale=False
		MaxParticles=300
		UniformSize=False
		StartSizeRange=(X=(Min=1.000000,Max=1.000000),Y=(Min=25.000000,Max=75.000000))
		Texture=Texture't_effect.particle.tracer_whizz'
		LifetimeRange=(Min=1.00000,Max=1.000000)
		StartVelocityRange=(X=(Min=0.000000,Max=0.000000),Y=(Min=0.000000,Max=0.000000),Z=(Min=-3096.000000,Max=-6000.000000))
		StartLocationRange=(X=(Min=-768.000000,Max=768.000000),Y=(Min=-768.000000,Max=768.000000),Z=(Max=0.000000))
		StartLocationOffset=(Z=3096.000000)
		RotationNormal=(X=0.00000,Y=0.00000,Z=1.00000)
		SecondsBeforeInactive=0
		RespawnDeadParticles=false
        ParticlesPerSecond=150.000000
        InitialParticlesPerSecond=150.000000
		AutomaticInitialSpawning=true
		DrawStyle=PTDS_AlphaBlend
		Opacity=0.25
    End Object

    Emitters=(SpriteEmitter'SpriteEmitter28')
	AutoReset=true
	AutoDestroy=false
	bStatic=false
	bNoDelete=false
	bHardAttach=true
	DrawScale=0.120000
}

class ExplosionDebris extends Emitter;



var int numBounces;

function PostBeginPlay()
{
	Velocity = vect(0,0,400) + 1000 * VRand();
	Velocity = 400 * Normal(Velocity);
	//EMStartVelocity = 0.3 * Velocity;
	SetTimer(3.0,false);
	Super.PostBeginPlay();
}

function Timer()
{
	Velocity = Velocity.Z * vect(0,0,1);
	numBounces = 5;
}

function HitWall( vector HitLocation, vector HitNormal, actor Wall )
{
	numBounces++;
	if ( numBounces > 4 )
	{
		//EMRespawnDeadParticles = false;
		if ( HitNormal.Z > 0 )
		{
			SetPhysics(PHYS_None);
			Velocity = vect(0,0,0);
		}
		return;
	}
	Velocity = (( Velocity dot HitNormal ) * HitNormal * (-2.0) + Velocity);   // Reflect off Wall w/damping
	if ( VSize(Velocity) > 300 )
		Velocity -= 0.2 * (HitNormal dot Velocity) * HitNormal;
	//EMStartVelocity = 0.3 * Velocity;
}

defaultproperties
{
	bDynamicLight=true
    LightType=LT_TexturePaletteOnce
    LightEffect=LE_NonIncidence
    LightBrightness=192
    LightHue=27
    LightSaturation=71
    LightRadius=3
	bUnlit=true
	bCollideWorld=true
	bBounce=True
    RemoteRole=ROLE_None
	Physics=PHYS_Falling
	bNoDelete=false
}

class gbxBloodEffect extends BloodEffectEmitter
	poolable( 0, 40 );

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx

simulated function PostNetBeginPlay()
{
	//log( self$"::PostNetBeginPlay() BloodDecalClass="$BloodDecalClass$" Location="$Location$" Rot="$Rotation$" HitX="$HitX$" HitY="$HitY$" HitZ="$HitZ );
	
	if ( Level.NetMode != NM_DedicatedServer )
		WallSplat();
	else 
		LifeSpan = 0.2;
}

simulated function WallSplat()
{
	local vector WallHit, WallNormal;
	local Actor WallActor;
	local vector HitDir;

	//log( self$"::WallSplat()BloodDecalClass="$BloodDecalClass$" Owner="$Owner$" HitX="$HitX$" HitY="$HitY$" HitZ="$HitZ );

	// The server creates his blood decal outside of this object.  See Pawn::PlayHit()
	if ( Level.NetMode != NM_Client )
		return;

	if ( Level.bDropDetail || (BloodDecalClass == None) )
		return;
	
	//log( self$"::WallSplat() Location="$Location$" Owner.Location="$Owner.Location );

	HitDir.X = HitX;
	HitDir.Y = HitY;
	HitDir.Z = HitZ;

	//log( self$"::WallSplat() set HitDir to float values HitDir="$HitDir$" HitX="$HitX$" HitY="$HitY$" HitZ="$HitZ );

	if ( HitDir == vect(0.0, 0.0, 0.0) )
		HitDir.Z = -1;

	WallActor = Trace(WallHit, WallNormal, Location + HitDir*-400, Location, false);

	//log( self$"::WallSplat() WallActor="$WallActor$" HitDir="$HitDir$" WallHit="$WallHit$" WallNormal="$WallNormal );

	if ( WallActor != None )
		spawn(BloodDecalClass,,,WallHit + 5 * (WallNormal + VRand()), rotator(-WallNormal));
}

//=============================================================================
// Configurable explosion trigger; drop one of these in your levels, set the
// effect type, the view shake parameters, and other things, and you're good to go.
//
// Author: Jeff Broome, Neil Johnson, Gearbox Software.
//=============================================================================
class gbxExplosionTrigger extends Trigger
	placeable;



//---------------------------------------------------------
// Variables
//---------------------------------------------------------
var() class<DamageType>	MyDamageType;
var() class<Emitter> ExplosionClass;
var   transient Actor	theExplosion;
var() float		Damage;
var() float		DamageRadius;
var() float		MomentumTransfer;		// Momentum magnitude imparted by impacting projectile.
var() float		ShakeRadius;			// radius within which to shake player views
var() float		ViewRollTime;			// how long to roll the instigator's view
var() float		RollMag;				// how far to roll view
var() float		RollRate;				// how fast to roll view
var() float		OffsetMagVertical;		// max view offset vertically
var() float		OffsetRateVertical;		// how fast to offset view vertically
var() float		OffsetMagHorizontal;	// max view offset horizontally
var() float		OffsetRateHorizontal;	// how fast to offset view horizontally
var() float		OffsetIterations;		// how many iterations to offset view
var() bool		bRetriggerable;			// This explosion trigger can be retriggered with the same emitter
var() name		szEmitterToUse;			// Set up an emitter we can use instead of creating our own.


//---------------------------------------------------------
// Explode
//---------------------------------------------------------
function Explode()
{
	local Controller C;
	local vector OffsetMag, OffsetRate;

	// shake the player's a bit...
	OffsetMag = OffsetMagHorizontal * vect(1,1,0) + OffsetMagVertical * vect(0,0,1);
	OffsetRate = OffsetRateHorizontal * vect(1,1,0) + OffsetRateVertical * vect(0,0,1);
	for ( C=Level.ControllerList; C!=None; C=C.NextController )
		if ( (PlayerController(C) != None) && (VSize(Location - PlayerController(C).ViewTarget.Location) < ShakeRadius) )
			C.ShakeView(ViewRollTime,RollMag,OffsetMag,RollRate,OffsetRate,OffsetIterations);

	// do the radius damage...
	HurtRadius(Damage, DamageRadius, MyDamageType, MomentumTransfer, Location );
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
// StartEffect
//---------------------------------------------------------
function StartEffect()
{
	local float Delay;
	local Actor Explosion;
	local Emitter anEmitter;
	local bool	fFound;

	log(self$".StartEffect() - "$Tag$" - "$ExplosionClass$" - "$theExplosion$" - "$Delay, 'EmitterCreate');
	// spawn the explosion effects...
	if (szEmitterToUse != '')
	{
		foreach DynamicActors( class'Emitter', anEmitter, szEmitterToUse )
		{
			break;
		}
		if (anEmitter != None)
		{
			Explosion = anEmitter;
			theExplosion = Explosion;
			theExplosion.SetLocation( Location );
			theExplosion.Trigger( None, None );
			fFound = true;
		}
	}
	if (!fFound && (ExplosionClass != None))
	{
//		if (bRetriggerable && !(ExplosionClass.Default.AutoDestroy))
		if (!(ExplosionClass.Default.AutoDestroy))
		{
			if (theExplosion == None)
			{
				Explosion = spawn(ExplosionClass, self,, Location, );
				theExplosion = Explosion;
			}
			else
			{
				Explosion = theExplosion;
				Explosion.Trigger( None, None );
			}
		}
		else
		{
			Explosion = spawn(ExplosionClass, self,, Location, );
		}
	}

	//log("NAJ**** "$theExplosion.Name$" ; "$theExplosion.Class.Name, 'naj');

	// This may be a delayed explosion, though.
	if ( Explosion.IsA( 'DelayedExplosion' ) )
	{
		//log("NAJ**** "$theExplosion.Name$" is a delayed explosion.", 'naj');
		Delay = DelayedExplosion( Explosion ).GetInitialDelay();
	}

	if ( Delay == 0.0 )
		Explode();
	else
		SetTimer( Delay, false );
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
// Timer
//---------------------------------------------------------
function Timer()
{
	Explode();
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
// Trigger
//---------------------------------------------------------
function Trigger( actor Other, pawn EventInstigator )
{
	StartEffect();
}

//=========================================================
//	Default Properties
//=========================================================
defaultproperties
{
	Damage=500.000000
	DamageRadius=512.000000
	MomentumTransfer=50000

	Texture=Texture'Engine.S_ExplosionTrigger'
	MyDamageType=class'DamageExplosionTrigger'
	ExplosionClass=class'gbxLandmineEffect'

    ShakeRadius=3000.000000
    ViewRollTime=0.250000
    RollMag=20.000000
    RollRate=100.000000
    OffsetMagVertical=20.000000
    OffsetRateVertical=1000.000000
    OffsetMagHorizontal=20.000000
    OffsetRateHorizontal=1000.000000
    OffsetIterations=10.000000

	RemoteRole=ROLE_AutonomousProxy
}
//=============================================================================
// Author: Stephen Palmer, Jeramy Cooke, Gearbox Software.
//=============================================================================
class gbxGrenadeExplosion extends Emitter
	transient;



simulated function PostBeginPlay()
{
	local int i;

	if ( Level.bDropDetail )
		LightRadius = 6;

	// Make sure sub-emitters will auto-destroy
	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		Emitters[i].AutoDestroy = true;
	}

	Super.PostBeginPlay();
}

defaultproperties
{
	AutoDestroy=true;
}
class gbxImpactEmitter extends Emitter
	transient
	poolable( 0, 20 );



//---------------------------------------------------------
// PostBeginPlay
//---------------------------------------------------------
function PostBeginPlay()
{
	local int i;
	local Vector ImpactRotVect;

	ImpactRotVect = Vector( Rotation + Rot(16384,0,0) );

	// Rotate emitter pitch 90 degrees
	// Make sure sub-emitters will auto-destroy
	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		Emitters[i].RotationNormal = ImpactRotVect;
		Emitters[i].AutoDestroy = true;
		if (Level.NetMode != NM_StandAlone)
		{
			Emitters[i].UseCollision = false;
		}
	}
}

defaultproperties
{
	bNoDelete=false
	bStatic=false
	AutoDestroy=true
	bLightChanged=true

	RemoteRole=ROLE_None
}

//*********************************************************
// gbxMuzzleFlash.uc
//
// Author: Neil Johnson
// 4/3/2003
//
// Base class for muzzle flash classes that use particle
// emitters.
//
//*********************************************************
class gbxMuzzleFlash extends Emitter
	abstract
	transient;

//---------------------------------------------------------
// Variables
//---------------------------------------------------------
var					int				TickCount;			// How long to display it
var					bool			bFireButtonDown;	// Is the fire button pressed?
var					bool			bLowDetail;			// Whether we're drawing w/ low framerate in mind.
var(MuzzleFlash)	ELightType		FlashLightType;
var(MuzzleFlash)	ELightEffect	FlashLightEffect;
var					array<RangeVector> BaseStartVelocityRange;

//*********************************************************
//	PostNetBeginPlay
//*********************************************************
simulated function PostNetBeginPlay()
{
	local int i;

	Super.PostNetBeginPlay();
	InitializeMuzzleFlash();	// Implementation-dependent.

	// Save the start velocity range vectors from each sub emitter, as they
	// may need to be modified with TriggerEmitters()
	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
		BaseStartVelocityRange[i] = Emitters[i].StartVelocityRange;
}

simulated function DisableZTest()
{
    local int i;
    for (i=0; i<Emitters.Length; ++i)
    {
        Emitters[i].ZTest = false;
        Emitters[i].ZWrite = false;
    }
}

//*********************************************************
//	Flash
//*********************************************************
simulated function Flash()
{
	if (!bFireButtonDown)
	{
		bFireButtonDown = true;
		FireButtonPressed();
	}

	ShowMuzzleFlash();	// Implementation-dependent.

	// Check to see if we need to low-detail the emitter
	// (because the framerate has dropped too low, for example).
	if( (Level.bDropDetail || Level.DetailMode == DM_Low))
	{
		if (!bLowDetail)
		{
			bLowDetail = true;
			AdjustForLowDetail();
		}
	}
	else
	if (bLowDetail)
	{
		bLowDetail = false;
		ResetToHighDetail();
	}

	// Make the muzzle flash visible.
	GotoState('Visible');
}

//*********************************************************
//	FiringStopped
//*********************************************************
function FiringStopped()
{

	bFireButtonDown = false;
	FireButtonReleased();
}

//*********************************************************
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Code for initializing your muzzle flash goes here.
//
function InitializeMuzzleFlash();

//*********************************************************
//	FireButtonPressed - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Code that should be executed when the user hits the fire
// button goes here.
//
function FireButtonPressed();

//*********************************************************
//	FireButtonReleased - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Code that should be executed when the user releases the
// fire button goes here.
//
function FireButtonReleased();

//*********************************************************
//	ShowMuzzleFlash - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Code that executes per each actual flash goes here.
//
simulated function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	local int i;

	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
//		if( i > 0 || Emitters[ 0 ].AllParticlesDead )
			Emitters[i].Trigger();
	}
}

//*********************************************************
//	HideMuzzleFlash - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Code that executes when each flash finishes goes here.
//
function HideMuzzleFlash();

//*********************************************************
//	AdjustForLowDetail - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Adjust the effect for a lower framerate here.
//
simulated function AdjustForLowDetail();

//*********************************************************
//	ResetToHighDetail - Implementation-dependent.
//*********************************************************
//
// Reset the changes made in AdjustForLowDetail() here.
//
simulated function ResetToHighDetail();

//*********************************************************
//	IsFlashing
//*********************************************************
//
// Report if the flash is currently active
//
function bool IsFlashing()
{
	local int i;

	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		if( !Emitters[i].AllParticlesDead )
			return true;
	}

	return false;
}

//##########################################################
//	Visible State
//##########################################################
simulated state Visible
{
	//*********************************************************
	//	Tick
	//*********************************************************
	simulated event Tick(float Delta)
	{
		if (TickCount>2)
			gotoState('');

		TickCount++;
	}

	//*********************************************************
	//	EndState
	//*********************************************************
	simulated function EndState()
	{
		// Hide the muzzle flash (Implementation-dependent).
		HideMuzzleFlash();

		LightEffect=LE_None;
		LightType=LT_None;
	}

	//*********************************************************
	//	BeginState
	//*********************************************************
	simulated function BeginState()
	{

		TickCount=0;

		LightEffect = FlashLightEffect;
		LightType = FlashLightType;
	}
}

//=========================================================
//	Default Properties
//=========================================================
defaultproperties
{
	bDynamicLight=True
	//FlashLightEffect=LE_NonIncidence
	//FlashLightType=LT_Steady
	FlashLightEffect=LE_None
	FlashLightType=LT_None
    LightBrightness=1024
    //LightHue=13
    LightSaturation=16
    LightRadius=8

	bStatic=false
	bNoDelete=false
	bHardAttach=true
	bOnlyDrawIfAttached=false
	//bTrailerSameRotation=true
	//Physics=PHYS_Trailer
}
//*********************************************************
// gbxRepeatableEmitter.uc
//
// Author: Stephen Palmer
// 10/25/2003
//
// Base class for emitters that are used to repeatedly spawn
// sub particles on demand.
//
//*********************************************************
class gbxRepeatableEmitter extends Emitter;



//-----------------------------
// Public variables
//-----------------------------
var string	EmitterSoundName;		// A sound to play with each trigger
var float	PlaySoundPct;			// Percentage of time to play the defined sound
var float	PawnVelocityFactor;		// Percentage of Instigator's velocity to add to sub emitter velocity

//-----------------------------
// Private fields
//-----------------------------
var Cue					EmitterSound;
var array<RangeVector>	BaseStartVelocityRange;

function PostBeginPlay()
{
	// Save the start velocity range vectors from each sub emitter, as they
	// may need to be modified with TriggerEmitters()

	local int i;

	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
		BaseStartVelocityRange[i] = Emitters[i].StartVelocityRange;
}

simulated function TriggerEmitters( Vector NewLocation, Rotator NewRotation )
{
	local float VelocityVal;
	local Vector PawnDirection, VelocityMod;
	local int i;
	local RangeVector NewStartVelocityRange;

	/// Play Sound
	if( frand() <= PlaySoundPct )
	{
		if( EmitterSound == None && EmitterSoundName != "" )
		{
			EmitterSound = LoadSound( EmitterSoundName );
		}

		if(EmitterSound != None )
		{
			PlaySoundCue( EmitterSound, SLOT_None );
		}
	}

	// Move the emitter into position
	SetLocation( NewLocation );
	//SetRotation( NewRotation );

	// Factor in the pawn's velocity
	if( (PawnVelocityFactor > 0.0f) && (Instigator != None) )
	{
		VelocityVal = PawnVelocityFactor * VSizeIgnoreZ(Instigator.Velocity);
		PawnDirection = Normal(Instigator.Velocity);

		VelocityMod.X = VelocityVal * PawnDirection dot Vector(Instigator.Rotation);
		VelocityMod.Y = VelocityVal * PawnDirection dot Vector(Instigator.Rotation + Rot(0, 16384, 0));
	}

	for( i = 0; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		if( Emitters[i].UseRotationFrom == PTRS_Offset )
			Emitters[i].RotationOffset = NewRotation;

		// Factor in the pawn's velocity
		if( PawnVelocityFactor > 0.0f )
		{
			NewStartVelocityRange = BaseStartVelocityRange[i];

			NewStartVelocityRange.X.Min += VelocityMod.X;
			NewStartVelocityRange.Y.Min += VelocityMod.Y;
			NewStartVelocityRange.X.Max += VelocityMod.X;
			NewStartVelocityRange.Y.Max += VelocityMod.Y;

			Emitters[i].StartVelocityRange = NewStartVelocityRange;
		}
		else
		{
			Emitters[i].StartVelocityRange = BaseStartVelocityRange[i];
		}

		Emitters[i].SpawnParticle(1);
	}
}

defaultproperties
{
	// Default properties
	PlaySoundPct=0.0
	PawnVelocityFactor=0.85

	// Set emitter class properties
	AutoDestroy=false
	AutoReset=true
	bNoDelete=false
	bHidden=false
}

//=============================================================================
// Bullet tracers glowing on the horizon.
//
// Author: Neil Johnson, Jeramy Cooke, Gearbox Software.
//=============================================================================
class HorizonTracers extends Actor placeable;




//---------------------------------------------------------
// Variables / Constants
//---------------------------------------------------------
var (HorizonTracers)	bool			bDisableTracers;
var (HorizonTracers)	float			PauseMin, PauseMax;		// In seconds, time between bursts.
var (HorizonTracers)	float			ThetaMin, ThetaMax;		// In degrees, angle of burst sweep.
var (HorizonTracers)	float			SpeedMin, SpeedMax;		// Degrees per second.
var (HorizonTracers)	class<Emitter>	EmitterClass;
var (HorizonTracers)	name			SoundProxyTag;			// Tag of actor that will emit sound for this gun
var						Sound			TracerFireLoop;
var						int				TracerFireLoopHandle;
var						Sound			TracerFireLastShot;
var						Actor			TracerTarget;			// If this actor exists, the tracers will aim at that target


var String LoopName, LastShotName;

var			Vector	AimVect;
var			Rotator	PitchOffset;
var			Rotator	YawOffset;
var			Rotator	AimRot;
var			float	SweepSpeed;
var			float	PauseLength;
var			float	Theta;
var const	float	TIME_SLICE;
var	transient	Emitter	HEmitter;
var			Actor	SoundProxy;

function PostBeginPlay()
{
	local Actor Proxy;

	foreach AllActors( class'Actor', Proxy, SoundProxyTag )
	{
		SoundProxy = Proxy;
		break;
	}

	if ( LoopName != "" )
	{
		TracerFireLoop = Sound( DynamicLoadObject( LoopName, class'Sound' ) );
	}

	if ( LastShotName != "" )
	{
		TracerFireLastShot = Sound( DynamicLoadObject( LastShotName, class'Sound' ) );
	}
}

function UpdateTracerTarget( Actor NewTarget )
{
	TracerTarget = NewTarget;
}

function RemoveTracerTarget()
{
	TracerTarget = None;
}

//=========================================================
//	State Firing
//=========================================================
auto state Firing
{

	//---------------------------------------------------------
	//	BeginState
	//---------------------------------------------------------
	function BeginState()
	{
		// Destroy the old emitter
		if( HEmitter != None )
		{
			HEmitter.Destroy();
			HEmitter = None;
		}

		// Spawn the emitter
		HEmitter = Spawn( EmitterClass );

		// Determine the sweep speed.
		SweepSpeed = ( SpeedMin + FRand() * (SpeedMax-SpeedMin) );

		// Determine the sweep angle and direction.
		Theta = ThetaMin + FRand() * (ThetaMax-ThetaMin);
		Theta = Clamp( Theta, 0, 359 );

		if( TracerTarget != None )
		{
			AimRot = Rotator( Normal(TracerTarget.Location - Location) );
			AimRot.Pitch = (AimRot.Pitch + 16384) & 65535;

			AimVect = Vector( AimRot );
		}
		else
		{
			YawOffset.Yaw = FRand() * 65535;

			// Take a vertical vector and pitch it backwards by 1/2 theta.
			PitchOffset.Pitch = 0.5 * (Theta * 65535/359);
			AimVect = Vect(1,0,0) >> PitchOffset >> YawOffset;
		}

		ApplyAimVect();
		TriggerTracers();

		// Trigger the start loop sound only if it's not already started
		//log("NAJ**** SoundProxy: "$SoundProxy.name$" ; TracerFireLoop: "$TracerFireLoop, 'naj');
		if (TracerFireLoopHandle == -1)
		{
			TracerFireLoopHandle = SoundProxy.PlaySound(TracerFireLoop, SLOT_None);
		}

		SetTimer( TIME_SLICE, true );
	}

	//---------------------------------------------------------
	//	Timer
	//---------------------------------------------------------
	function Timer()
	{
		local float DeltaSweep;
		//log("NAJ**** Firing::Timer().");

		if ( Theta <= 0.0 || bDisableTracers )
		{
			SetTimer( 0.0, false );
			GotoState( 'Pausing' );

			// Stop the loop sound to avoid stacking up sounds since the Pausing state will restart a Firing state
			if (TracerFireLoopHandle != -1)
			{
				SoundProxy.StopSound(TracerFireLoopHandle);
				TracerFireLoopHandle = -1;
			}

			// Trigger the end sound
			SoundProxy.PlaySound(TracerFireLastShot, SLOT_None);

			SuspendTracers();
		}
		else
		{
			// Adjust the firing angle.
			DeltaSweep = SweepSpeed * TIME_SLICE;
			Theta -= DeltaSweep;

			if( TracerTarget != None )
			{
				AimRot = Rotator( Normal(TracerTarget.Location - Location) );
				AimRot.Pitch = (AimRot.Pitch + 16384) & 65535;

				AimVect = Vector( AimRot );
				//AimVect = Normal( TracerTarget.Location - Location ) >> Rot( 0, 32768, 0 );
			}
			else
			{
				PitchOffset.Pitch -= (DeltaSweep * 65535/359);
				AimVect = Vect(1,0,0) >> PitchOffset >> YawOffset;
			}

			ApplyAimVect();
		}
	}
}

//=========================================================
//	State Pausing
//=========================================================
state Pausing
{
	//---------------------------------------------------------
	//	BeginState
	//---------------------------------------------------------
	function BeginState()
	{
		//log("NAJ**** Pausing::BeginState().");

		// Determine pause time.
		PauseLength = PauseMin + FRand() * (PauseMax-PauseMin);
		SetTimer( PauseLength, false );
	}

	//---------------------------------------------------------
	//	Timer
	//---------------------------------------------------------
	function Timer()
	{
		//log("NAJ**** Pausing::Timer().");
		Super.Timer();
		
		if ( !bDisableTracers )
		{
			GotoState( 'Firing' );
		}
		else
		{
			SetTimer( 0.5, false );
		}
	}
}

function ApplyAimVect()
{
	local int i;

	if( HEmitter == None )
	{
		return;
	}
	
	for( i = 0; i < HEmitter.Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		HEmitter.Emitters[i].RotationNormal = AimVect;
	}
}

function TriggerTracers()
{
	local int i;

	if( HEmitter == None )
	{
		// Spawn the emitter
		HEmitter = Spawn( EmitterClass );
	}

	for( i = 0; i < HEmitter.Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		HEmitter.Emitters[i].Trigger();
	}
}

function SuspendTracers()
{
	local int i;

	if( HEmitter == None )
	{
		return;
	}
	
	for( i = 0; i < HEmitter.Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		HEmitter.Emitters[i].SuspendSpawning();
	}
}

function StopTracers()
{
	bDisableTracers = true;
}

function RestartTracers()
{
	bDisableTracers = false;
}

function ToggleStopTracers()
{
	bDisableTracers = !bDisableTracers;
}

function Trigger( actor Other, pawn EventInstigator )
{
	ToggleStopTracers();
}

//=========================================================
//	Default Properties
//=========================================================
defaultproperties
{
	bHidden=true
	bNoDelete=false
	bStatic=false
	RemoteRole=ROLE_AutonomousProxy

	PauseMin=1.0
	PauseMax=2.0
	SpeedMin=45.0
	SpeedMax=45.0
	ThetaMin=30
	ThetaMax=70
	TIME_SLICE=0.5

	EmitterClass=class'EmitterHorizonTracers'
	//TracerFireLoop=Sound'D20630_SOUNDS.ANTIAIR_LOOP'
	//TracerFireLastShot=Sound'D20630_SOUNDS.ANTIAIR_STOP'
//	LoopName="D20630_SOUNDS.ANTIAIR_LOOP"
//	LastShotName="D20630_SOUNDS.ANTIAIR_STOP"
	TracerFireLoopHandle=-1
}

class MuzzleFlashFlakvierling extends gbxMuzzleFlash
	poolable( 21, 0 );

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function InitializeMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	ShowMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	//Only trigger the non smoke effects.
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = false;
	Emitters[1].Trigger();
	Emitters[2].Trigger();
	Emitters[3].Trigger();
}

//	Default Properties
//=========================================================

//=============================================================================
// Muzzle flash effect for the German MG42 machine gun.
//
// Author: Neil Johnson, Gearbox Software.
//=============================================================================
class MuzzleFlashMG42_ extends gbxMuzzleFlash
	poolable( 12, 0 );

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx



//---------------------------------------------------------
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function InitializeMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	ShowMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[1].Trigger();
	Emitters[1].Trigger();
	//Emitters[2].Trigger();
	//Emitters[3].Trigger();
	//Emitters[4].Trigger();
	//Emitters[5].Trigger();
	//Emitters[6].Trigger();
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	HideMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function HideMuzzleFlash()
{	
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonPressed
//---------------------------------------------------------
function FireButtonPressed()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = false;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonReleased
//---------------------------------------------------------
function FireButtonReleased()
{
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

class MuzzleFlashPak88_ extends gbxMuzzleFlash
	poolable( 21, 0 );

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function InitializeMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	ShowMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	//Only trigger the non smoke effects.
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = false;
	Emitters[1].Trigger();
	Emitters[2].Trigger();
	Emitters[3].Trigger();
}

	transient;

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx



//---------------------------------------------------------
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function InitializeMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	ShowMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	local int i;

	for( i = 1; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		Emitters[i].Trigger();
	}
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	HideMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function HideMuzzleFlash()
{
}

//	FireButtonPressed
//---------------------------------------------------------

{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = false;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonReleased
//---------------------------------------------------------

{
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//=============================================================================
// Muzzle flash effect for the Stuart Tank bow machine gun
//=============================================================================
class MuzzleFlashStuartTankBowGun extends gbxMuzzleFlash
	transient;

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx



//---------------------------------------------------------
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function InitializeMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	ShowMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	local int i;

	for( i = 1; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		Emitters[i].Trigger();
	}
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	HideMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function HideMuzzleFlash()
{
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonPressed
//---------------------------------------------------------
function FireButtonPressed()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = false;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonReleased
//---------------------------------------------------------
function FireButtonReleased()
{
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//	Default Properties
//=========================================================

//=============================================================================
// Muzzle flash effect for the Stuart Tank bow machine gun
//=============================================================================
class MuzzleFlashStuartTankCoaxGun extends gbxMuzzleFlash
	transient;

#exec OBJ LOAD FILE=..\texture\t_effect.utx



//---------------------------------------------------------
//	InitializeMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function InitializeMuzzleFlash()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	ShowMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function ShowMuzzleFlash()
{
	local int i;

	for( i = 1; i < Emitters.Length; i++ )
	{
		Emitters[i].Trigger();
	}
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	HideMuzzleFlash
//---------------------------------------------------------
function HideMuzzleFlash()
{
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonPressed
//---------------------------------------------------------
function FireButtonPressed()
{
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].Trigger();
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = false;
}

//---------------------------------------------------------
//	FireButtonReleased
//---------------------------------------------------------
function FireButtonReleased()
{
	Emitters[0].bSuspendSpawning = true;
}

class ProjectorRelative extends Projector
    native;

var actor   RelParent;
var vector  RelLocation;
var rotator RelRotation;
var int     RelRoll;    // Roll is destroyed due to the math and must be explicitly managed
var float	RelParentSetTime;  // keep track of when Parent was set so we can remove the oldest one when there's too many


simulated native function SetRelativeProjector(actor Parent, optional vector WorldSpacePosition, optional rotator WorldSpaceRotation);
simulated native function UpdateRelativeProjector();

simulated function Tick(float DeltaTime)
{
    Super.Tick(DeltaTime);
    if (RelParent != None)
    {
        UpdateRelativeProjector();
    	DetachProjector();
    	AttachProjector(RelParent);
    }
}

defaultproperties
{
	bStatic=False

	bProjFlag_Shadow=False
	bProjFlag_VehicleShadow=False
	bProjFlag_LevelShadow=False
	bProjFlag_Blood=False
	bProjFlag_Bullet=False
	bProjFlag_Blast=False
	bProjFlag_SAVIcon=False
	bProjFlag_ObjectiveIcon=False
	bProjFlag_CommandRing=False
}
//=============================================================================
// scorch
// base class of Warfare damage decals
//=============================================================================
class Scorch extends Projector;



var() float Lifetime;
var() float PushBack;
var() bool  RandomOrient;
var config bool  bDecalsEnabled;

function PostBeginPlay()
{
    local Vector RX, RY, RZ;
    local Rotator R;

    if ( !bDecalsEnabled || Level.NetMode == NM_DedicatedServer )
    {
        Destroy();
        return;
    }

    if ( RandomOrient )
    {
        R.Yaw = 0;
        R.Pitch = 0;
        R.Roll = FRand() * 65535;
        GetAxes(R,RX,RY,RZ);
        RX = RX >> Rotation;
        RY = RY >> Rotation;
        RZ = RZ >> Rotation;
        R = OrthoRotation(RX,RY,RZ);
        SetRotation(R);
    }

    SetLocation( Location - Vector(Rotation)*PushBack );

    Super.PostBeginPlay();
    AbandonProjector(Lifetime);
    Destroy();
}

/* Reset()
reset actor to initial state - used when restarting level without reloading.
*/
function Reset()
{
	Destroy();
}

defaultproperties
{
	BlendEquation=blendequation_Add
	BlendSrcFunction=blend_DstColor
	BlendDstFunction=blend_SrcColor
	bDoNotColorFog=false
	bDoNotAlphaFog=false
	bOverrideFogColor=true
	TransparentFactor=(R=0,G=0,B=0,A=255)
	TransparentColor=(R=128,G=128,B=128,A=255)
	OverriddenFogColor=(R=128,G=128,B=128,A=255)
	
	FOV=1
	MaxTraceDistance=64
	bProjectBSP=true
	bProjectTerrain=true
	bProjectStaticMesh=true
	bProjectActor=false

	bClipBSP=true
	bClipStaticMesh=True
	bClipStaticMeshTris=True

    bNoDelete=false
    bStatic=false

	Lifetime=45
    PushBack=24
    RandomOrient=true
    bDecalsEnabled=true

	bProjFlag_Shadow=False
	bProjFlag_VehicleShadow=False
	bProjFlag_LevelShadow=False
	bProjFlag_Blood=False
	bProjFlag_Bullet=True
	bProjFlag_Blast=False
	bProjFlag_SAVIcon=False
	bProjFlag_ObjectiveIcon=False
	bProjFlag_CommandRing=False

	bDeleteSimple=true
}
